Accepts <a href="#page:home,header:home-pagination">Pagination parameters</a>.</p>
<section id="marketplace-list-orders-get" class="panel panel-info"><div class="panel-heading"><div style="float:right"><span style="text-transform: lowercase; display: none">List Orders</span></div><div style="float:left"><a href="#page:marketplace,header:marketplace-list-orders-get" class="btn btn-xs btn-primary">GET</a></div><div style="overflow:hidden"><code>/marketplace/orders{?status,created_after,created_before,sort,sort_order}</code></div></div><div class="panel-body"><p>Returns a list of the authenticated user’s orders. Accepts <a href="#page:home,header:home-pagination">Pagination parameters</a>.</p>
</div><ul class="list-group"><li class="list-group-item bg-default"><strong>Parameters</strong></li><li class="list-group-item"><dl class="dl-horizontal"><dt>status</dt><dd><code>string</code>&nbsp;<span>(optional)</span>&nbsp;<span class="text-muted example"><strong>Example:&nbsp;</strong><span>1-1</span></span><p>Only show orders with this status. Valid <code>status</code> keys are:    <br />
<code>All</code><br>
<code>New Order</code><br>
<code>Buyer Contacted</code><br>
<code>Invoice Sent</code><br>
<code>Payment Pending</code><br>
<code>Payment Received</code>
<code>In Progress</code>
<code>Shipped</code><br>
<code>Merged</code><br>
<code>Order Changed</code><br>
<code>Refund Sent</code><br>
<code>Cancelled</code><br>
<code>Cancelled (Non-Paying Buyer)</code><br>
<code>Cancelled (Item Unavailable)</code><br>
<code>Cancelled (Per Buyer's Request)</code>
<code>Cancelled (Refund Received)</code></p>
</dd><dt>created_after</dt><dd><code>string</code>&nbsp;<span>(optional)</span>&nbsp;<span class="text-muted example"><strong>Example:&nbsp;</strong><span>2019-06-24T20:58:58Z</span></span><p>Only show orders created after this ISO 8601 timestamp.</p>
</dd><dt>created_before</dt><dd><code>string</code>&nbsp;<span>(optional)</span>&nbsp;<span class="text-muted example"><strong>Example:&nbsp;</strong><span>2019-06-24T20:58:58Z</span></span><p>Only show orders created before this ISO 8601 timestamp.</p>
</dd><dt>archived</dt><dd><code>boolean</code>&nbsp;<span>(optional)</span>&nbsp;<span class="text-muted example"><strong>Example:&nbsp;</strong><span>true</span></span><p>Only show orders with a specific archived status. If no key is provided, both statuses are returned. Valid <code>archived</code> keys are:    <br />
<code>true</code><br>
<code>false</code></p>
</dd><dt>sort</dt><dd><code>string</code>&nbsp;<span>(optional)</span>&nbsp;<span class="text-muted example"><strong>Example:&nbsp;</strong><span>1-1</span></span><p>Sort items by this field (see below). Valid <code>sort</code> keys are:    <br />
<code>id</code><br>
<code>buyer</code><br>
<code>created</code><br>
<code>status</code><br>
<code>last_activity</code></p>
</dd><dt>sort_order</dt><dd><code>string</code>&nbsp;<span>(optional)</span>&nbsp;<span class="text-muted example"><strong>Example:&nbsp;</strong><span>1-1</span></span><p>Sort items in a particular order (one of <code>asc</code>, <code>desc</code>)</p>
</dd></dl></li></ul><ul class="list-group"><li class="list-group-item"><strong>Response&nbsp;&nbsp;<code>200</code></strong><button data-toggle="collapse" data-target="#768514c1ce91e5f54e5749cc740b3506" type="button" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="768514c1ce91e5f54e5749cc740b3506" class="pull-right toggle-button">Toggle</button></li><li id="768514c1ce91e5f54e5749cc740b3506" class="list-group-item panel-collapse collapse"><div class="description"></div><h5>Headers</h5><pre><code><span class="hljs-attribute">Status</span>: <span class="hljs-string">HTTP/1.1 200 OK</span><br><span class="hljs-attribute">Reproxy-Status</span>: <span class="hljs-string">yes</span><br><span class="hljs-attribute">Access-Control-Allow-Origin</span>: <span class="hljs-string">*</span><br><span class="hljs-attribute">Cache-Control</span>: <span class="hljs-string">public, must-revalidate</span><br><span class="hljs-attribute">Content-Type</span>: <span class="hljs-string">application/json</span><br><span class="hljs-attribute">Server</span>: <span class="hljs-string">lighttpd</span><br><span class="hljs-attribute">Content-Length</span>: <span class="hljs-string">780</span><br><span class="hljs-attribute">Date</span>: <span class="hljs-string">Tue, 15 Jul 2014 19:59:59 GMT</span><br><span class="hljs-attribute">X-Varnish</span>: <span class="hljs-string">1702965334</span><br><span class="hljs-attribute">Age</span>: <span class="hljs-string">0</span><br><span class="hljs-attribute">Via</span>: <span class="hljs-string">1.1 varnish</span><br><span class="hljs-attribute">Connection</span>: <span class="hljs-string">keep-alive</span><br></code></pre><h5>Body</h5><pre><code>{

When posting a new message, you can simultaneously change the order status. If you do, the message will automatically be prepended with:<br>
<code>Seller changed status from Old Status to New Status</code><br>
While <code>message</code> and <code>status</code> are each optional, one or both must be present.</p>

</span>}</code></pre></li></ul></section><h2 id="marketplace-release-statistics">Release Statistics&nbsp;<a href="#page:marketplace,header:marketplace-release-statistics"><i class="fa fa-link"></i></a></h2><section id="marketplace-release-statistics-get" class="panel panel-info"><div class="panel-heading"><div style="float:right"><span style="text-transform: lowercase; display: none">Get Marketplace Stats</span></div><div style="float:left"><a href="#page:marketplace,header:marketplace-release-statistics-get" class="btn btn-xs btn-primary">GET</a></div><div style="overflow:hidden"><code>/marketplace/stats/{release_id}{?curr_abbr}</code></div></div><div class="panel-body"><p>Retrieve marketplace statistics for the provided Release ID. These statistics reflect the state of the release in the marketplace <em>currently</em>, and include the number of items currently for sale, lowest listed price of any item for sale, and whether the item is blocked for sale in the marketplace.</p>
<p><a href="#page:authentication">Authentication</a> is optional. Authenticated users will by default have the lowest currency expressed in their own buyer currency, configurable in <a href="https://www.discogs.com/settings/buyer">buyer settings</a>, in the absence of the <code>curr_abbr</code> query parameter to specify the currency.
Unauthenticated users will have the price expressed in US Dollars, if no <code>curr_abbr</code> is provided.</p>
<p>Releases that have no items for sale in the marketplace will return a body with null data in the <code>lowest_price</code> and <code>num_for_sale</code> keys. Releases that are blocked for sale will also have null data for these keys.</p>
</div><ul class="list-group"><li class="list-group-item bg-default"><strong>Parameters</strong></li><li class="list-group-item"><dl class="dl-horizontal"><dt>release_id</dt><dd><code>number</code>&nbsp;<span class="required">(required)</span>&nbsp;<span class="text-muted example"><strong>Example:&nbsp;</strong><span>1</span></span><p>The release ID whose stats are desired</p>
</dd><dt>curr_abbr</dt><dd><code>string</code>&nbsp;<span>(optional)</span>&nbsp;<span class="text-muted example"><strong>Example:&nbsp;</strong><span>USD</span></span><p>Currency for marketplace data. Defaults to the authenticated users currency. Must be one of the following:    <br />
<code>USD</code>
<code>GBP</code>
<code>EUR</code>
<code>CAD</code>
<code>AUD</code>
<code>JPY</code>
<code>CHF</code>
<code>MXN</code>
<code>BRL</code>
<code>NZD</code>
<code>SEK</code>
<code>ZAR</code></p>
</dd></dl></li></ul><ul class="list-group"><li class="list-group-item"><strong>Response&nbsp;&nbsp;<code>200</code></strong><button data-toggle="collapse" data-target="#bc047ccb4d7ae19fdcf83e2b13f04403" type="button" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="bc047ccb4d7ae19fdcf83e2b13f04403" class="pull-right toggle-button">Toggle</button></li><li id="bc047ccb4d7ae19fdcf83e2b13f04403" class="list-group-item panel-collapse collapse"><div class="description"></div><h5>Headers</h5><pre><code><span class="hljs-attribute">Status</span>: <span class="hljs-string">HTTP/1.1 200 OK</span><br><span class="hljs-attribute">Reproxy-Status</span>: <span class="hljs-string">yes</span><br><span class="hljs-attribute">Access-Control-Allow-Origin</span>: <span class="hljs-string">*</span><br><span class="hljs-attribute">Cache-Control</span>: <span class="hljs-string">public, must-revalidate</span><br><span class="hljs-attribute">Content-Type</span>: <span class="hljs-string">application/json</span><br><span class="hljs-attribute">Server</span>: <span class="hljs-string">lighttpd</span><br><span class="hljs-attribute">Content-Length</span>: <span class="hljs-string">780</span><br><span class="hljs-attribute">Date</span>: <span class="hljs-string">Tue, 15 Jul 2014 19:59:59 GMT</span><br><span class="hljs-attribute">X-Varnish</span>: <span class="hljs-string">1702965334</span><br><span class="hljs-attribute">Age</span>: <span class="hljs-string">0</span><br><span class="hljs-attribute">Via</span>: <span class="hljs-string">1.1 varnish</span><br><span class="hljs-attribute">Connection</span>: <span class="hljs-string">keep-alive</span><br></code></pre><h5>Body</h5><pre><code>{
  "<span class="hljs-attribute">lowest_price</span>": <span class="hljs-value">{
    "<span class="hljs-attribute">currency</span>": <span class="hljs-value"><span class="hljs-string">"USD"</span></span>,
    "<span class="hljs-attribute">value</span>": <span class="hljs-value"><span class="hljs-number">2.09</span>
  </span>}</span>,
  "<span class="hljs-attribute">num_for_sale</span>": <span class="hljs-value"><span class="hljs-number">26</span></span>,
  "<span class="hljs-attribute">blocked_from_sale</span>": <span class="hljs-value"><span class="hljs-literal">false</span>
</span>}</code></pre></li></ul></section></div></div><a href="#page:inventory-export" class="btn btn-default pull-right">Next&nbsp;<i class="fa fa-arrow-circle-right"></i></a><a href="#page:images" class="btn btn-default"><i class="fa fa-arrow-circle-left"></i> Previous</a><div class="clearfix"></div><hr></div><div data-bind="visible: page() == 'inventory-export', style: {marginTop: page() == 'inventory-export' ? </dd></dl></li></ul><ul class="list-group"><li class="list-group-item"><strong>Response&nbsp;&nbsp;<code>200</code></strong><button data-toggle="collapse" data-target="#ee682ebe65e7bdb8ca915377975ee425" type="button" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="ee682ebe65e7bdb8ca915377975ee425" class="pull-right toggle-button">Toggle</button></li><li id="ee682ebe65e7bdb8ca915377975ee425" class="list-group-item panel-collapse collapse"><div class="description"></div><h5>Headers</h5><pre><code><span class="hljs-attribute">Content-Type</span>: <span class="hljs-string">text/csv; charset=utf-8</span><br><span class="hljs-attribute">Content-Disposition</span>: <span class="hljs-string">attachment; filename=cburmeister-inventory-20180927-1259.csv</span><br></code></pre></li><li class="list-group-item"><strong>Response&nbsp;&nbsp;<code>401</code></strong><button data-toggle="collapse" data-target="#c93ffda9c20db37395168c27a5059de5" type="button" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="c93ffda9c20db37395168c27a5059de5" class="pull-right toggle-button">Toggle</button></li><li id="c93ffda9c20db37395168c27a5059de5" class="list-group-item panel-collapse collapse"><div class="description"></div><h5>Headers</h5><pre><code><span class="hljs-attribute">Content-Type</span>: <span class="hljs-string">application/json</span><br></code></pre></li><li class="list-group-item"><strong>Response&nbsp;&nbsp;<code>404</code></strong><button data-toggle="collapse" data-target="#cdca5d371d57824c77bf08a3742464e5" type="button" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="cdca5d371d57824c77bf08a3742464e5" class="pull-right toggle-button">Toggle</button></li><li id="cdca5d371d57824c77bf08a3742464e5" class="list-group-item panel-collapse collapse"><div class="description"></div><h5>Headers</h5><pre><code><span class="hljs-attribute">Content-Type</span>: <span class="hljs-string">application/json</span><br></code></pre></li></ul></section></div></div><a href="#page:inventory-upload" class="btn btn-default pull-right">Next&nbsp;<i class="fa fa-arrow-circle-right"></i></a><a href="#page:marketplace" class="btn btn-default"><i class="fa fa-arrow-circle-left"></i> Previous</a><div class="clearfix"></div><hr></div><div data-bind="visible: page() == 'inventory-upload', style: {marginTop: page() == 'inventory-upload' ? '38px' : ''}"><div class="panel panel-default"><div class="panel-heading"><h1 id="inventory-upload" class="panel-heading-title">Inventory Upload&nbsp;<a href="#page:inventory-upload"><i class="fa fa-link"></i></a></h1></div><div class="panel-body"><h2 id="inventory-upload-add-inventory">Add inventory&nbsp;<a href="#page:inventory-upload,header:inventory-upload-add-inventory"><i class="fa fa-link"></i></a></h2><section id="inventory-upload-add-inventory-post" class="panel panel-success"><div class="panel-heading"><div style="float:right"><span style="text-transform: lowercase; display: none">Add inventory</span></div><div style="float:left"><a href="#page:inventory-upload,header:inventory-upload-add-inventory-post" class="btn btn-xs btn-success">POST</a></div><div style="overflow:hidden"><code>/inventory/upload/add</code></div></div><div class="panel-body"><p>Upload a CSV of listings to add to your inventory.</p>
<h3 id="header-file-structure">File structure <a class="permalink" href="#header-file-structure" aria-hidden="true">¶</a></h3>
<p>The file you upload must be a comma-separated CSV. The first row must be a
header with lower case field names.</p>
<p>Here’s an example:</p>
<pre><code>release_id,price,media_condition,comments
123,1.50,Mint (<span class="hljs-keyword">M</span>),Comments <span class="hljs-keyword">about</span> this release <span class="hljs-keyword">for</span> sale
456,2.50,Near Mint (NM or <span class="hljs-keyword">M</span>-),<span class="hljs-keyword">More</span> comments
7890,3.50,Good (<span class="hljs-keyword">G</span>),Signed vinyl <span class="hljs-keyword">copy</span></code></pre>
<h3 id="header-things-to-note-">Things to note: <a class="permalink" href="#header-things-to-note-" aria-hidden="true">¶</a></h3>
<p>These listings will be marked “For Sale” immediately. Currency information will
be pulled from your marketplace settings. Any fields that aren’t optional or
required will be ignored.</p>
<h3 id="header-required-fields">Required fields <a class="permalink" href="#header-required-fields" aria-hidden="true">¶</a></h3>
<ul>
<li>
<p><code>release_id</code> - Must be a number. This value corresponds with the Discogs
database Release ID.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><code>price</code> - Must be a number.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><code>media_condition</code> - Must be a valid condition (see below).</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h3 id="header-optional-fields">Optional fields <a class="permalink" href="#header-optional-fields" aria-hidden="true">¶</a></h3>
<ul>
<li>
<p><code>sleeve_condition</code> - Must be a valid condition (see below).</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><code>comments</code>
<code>accept_offer</code> - Must be Y or N.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><code>location</code> - Private free-text field to help identify an item’s physical
location.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><code>external_id</code> - Private notes or IDs for your own reference.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><code>weight</code> - In grams. Must be a non-negative integer.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><code>format_quantity</code> - Number of items that this item counts as (for shipping).</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h3 id="header-conditions">Conditions <a class="permalink" href="#header-conditions" aria-hidden="true">¶</a></h3>
<p>When you specify a media condition, it must exactly match one of these:</p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><code>Mint (M)</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><code>Near Mint (NM or M-)</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><code>Very Good Plus (VG+)</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><code>Very Good (VG)</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><code>Good Plus (G+)</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><code>Good (G)</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><code>Fair (F)</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><code>Poor (P)</code></p>
</li>
</ul>
<p>Sleeve condition may be any of the above, or:</p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><code>Not Graded</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><code>Generic</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><code>No Cover</code></p>
</li>
</ul>
</div><ul class="list-group"><li class="list-group-item bg-default"><strong>Parameters</strong></li><li class="list-group-item"><dl class="dl-horizontal"><dt>upload</dt><dd><code>file</code>&nbsp;<span class="required">(required)</span>&nbsp;<p>The CSV file of items to add to your inventory.</p>
</dd></dl></li></ul><ul class="list-group"><li class="list-group-item"><strong>Response&nbsp;&nbsp;<code>200</code></strong><button data-toggle="collapse" class="description"></div><h5>Headers</h5><pre><code><span class="hljs-attribute">Content-Type</span>: <span class="hljs-string">application/json</span><br></code></pre></li></ul></section><h2 id="inventory-upload-change-inventory">Change inventory&nbsp;<a href="#page:inventory-upload,header:inventory-upload-change-inventory"><i class="fa fa-link"></i></a></h2><section id="inventory-upload-change-inventory-post" class="panel panel-success"><div class="panel-heading"><div style="float:right"><span style="text-transform: lowercase; display: none">Change inventory</span></div><div style="float:left"><a href="#page:inventory-upload,header:inventory-upload-change-inventory-post" class="btn btn-xs btn-success">POST</a></div><div style="overflow:hidden"><code>/inventory/upload/change</code></div></div><div class="panel-body"><p>Upload a CSV of listings to change in your inventory.</p>
<h3 id="header-file-structure-1">File structure <a class="permalink" href="#header-file-structure-1" aria-hidden="true">¶</a></h3>
<p>The file you upload must be a comma-separated CSV. The first row must be a
header with lower case field names.</p>
<p>Here’s an example:</p>
<pre><code>release_id,price,media_condition,comments
123,1.50,Mint (<span class="hljs-keyword">M</span>),Comments <span class="hljs-keyword">about</span> this release <span class="hljs-keyword">for</span> sale
456,2.50,Near Mint (NM or <span class="hljs-keyword">M</span>-),<span class="hljs-keyword">More</span> comments
7890,3.50,Good (<span class="hljs-keyword">G</span>),Signed vinyl <span class="hljs-keyword">copy</span></code></pre>
<h3 id="header-things-to-note--1">Things to note: <a class="permalink" href="#header-things-to-note--1" aria-hidden="true">¶</a></h3>
<p>These listings will be marked “For Sale” immediately. Currency information will
be pulled from your marketplace settings. Any fields that aren’t optional or
required will be ignored.</p>
<h3 id="header-required-fields-1">Required fields <a class="permalink" href="#header-required-fields-1" aria-hidden="true">¶</a></h3>
<ul>
<li><code>release_id</code> - Must be a number. This value corresponds with the Discogs
database Release ID.</li>
</ul>
<h2 id="header-optional-fields-(at-least-one-required)">Optional fields (at least one required) <a class="permalink" href="#header-optional-fields-(at-least-one-required)" aria-hidden="true">¶</a></h2>
<ul>
<li>
<p><code>price</code> -</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><code>media_condition</code> - Must be a valid condition (see below).</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><code>sleeve_condition</code> - Must be a valid condition (see below).</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><code>comments</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><code>accept_offer</code> - Must be Y or N.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><code>external_id</code> - Private notes or IDs for your own reference.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><code>location</code> - Private free-text field to help identify an item’s physical
location.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><code>weight</code> - In grams. Must be a non-negative integer.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><code>format_quantity</code> - Number of items that this item counts as (for shipping).</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h3 id="header-conditions-1">Conditions <a class="permalink" href="#header-conditions-1" aria-hidden="true">¶</a></h3>
<p>When you specify a media condition, it must exactly match one of these:</p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><code>Mint (M)</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><code>Near Mint (NM or M-)</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><code>Very Good Plus (VG+)</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><code>Very Good (VG)</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><code>Good Plus (G+)</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><code>Good (G)</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><code>Fair (F)</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><code>Poor (P)</code></p>
</li>
</ul>
<p>Sleeve condition may be any of the above, or:</p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><code>Not Graded</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><code>Generic</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p><code>No Cover</code></p>
</li>
</ul>
</div><ul class="list-group"><li class="list-group-item bg-default"><strong>Parameters</strong></li><li class="list-group-item"><dl class="dl-horizontal"><dt>upload</dt><dd><code>file</code>&nbsp;<span class="required">(required)</span>&nbsp;<p>The CSV file of items to alter in your inventory.</p>
</dd></dl></li></ul><ul class="list-group"><li class="list-group-item"><strong>Response&nbsp;&nbsp;<code>200</code></strong><button data-toggle="collapse" data-target="#d20e80ee94c25f6d938acf8f47eaa7cf" type="button" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="d20e80ee94c25f6d938acf8f47eaa7cf" class="pull-right toggle-button">Toggle</button></li><li id="d20e80ee94c25f6d938acf8f47eaa7cf" class="list-group-item panel-collapse collapse"><div class="description"></div><h5>Headers</h5><pre><code><span class="hljs-attribute">Content-Type</span>: <span class="hljs-string">application/json</span><br><span class="hljs-attribute">Location</span>: <span class="hljs-string">https://api.discogs.com/inventory/upload/599632</span><br></code></pre></li><li aria-controls="49d17e4cc3960516d1c283a3b7dd9af0" class="pull-right toggle-button">Toggle</button></li><li id="49d17e4cc3960516d1c283a3b7dd9af0" class="list-group-item panel-collapse collapse"><div If authenticated as the requested user, the <code>email</code> key will be visible,
and the <code>num_list</code> count will include the user’s private lists.<br>
If authenticated as the requested user or the user’s collection/wantlist is public, the <code>num_collection</code> / <code>num_wantlist</code> keys will be visible.</p>

<section id="user-identity-user-submissions-get" class="panel panel-info"><div class="panel-heading"><div style="float:right"><span style="text-transform: lowercase; display: none">Get Submissions</span></div><div style="float:left"><a href="#page:user-identity,header:user-identity-user-submissions-get" class="btn btn-xs btn-primary">GET</a></div><div style="overflow:hidden"><code>/users/{username}/submissions</code></div></div><div class="panel-body"><p>Retrieve a user’s submissions by username. Accepts <a href="#page:home,header:home-pagination">Pagination</a> parameters.</p>
</div><ul class="list-group"><li class="list-group-item bg-default"><strong>Parameters</strong></li><li class="list-group-item"><dl class="dl-horizontal"><dt>username</dt><dd><code>string</code>&nbsp;<span class="required">(required)</span>&nbsp;<span class="text-muted example"><strong>Example:&nbsp;</strong><span>shooezgirl</span></span><p>The username of the submissions you are trying to fetch.</p>

<section id="user-identity-user-contributions-get" class="panel panel-info"><div class="panel-heading"><div style="float:right"><span style="text-transform: lowercase; display: none">Get Contributions</span></div><div style="float:left"><a href="#page:user-identity,header:user-identity-user-contributions-get" class="btn btn-xs btn-primary">GET</a></div><div style="overflow:hidden"><code>/users/{username}/contributions{?sort,sort_order}</code></div></div><div class="panel-body"><p>Retrieve a user’s contributions by username. Accepts <a href="#page:home,header:home-pagination">Pagination</a> parameters.</p>
<p>Valid <code>sort</code> keys are:<br>
<code>label</code><br>
<code>artist</code><br>
<code>title</code><br>
<code>catno</code><br>
<code>format</code><br>
<code>rating</code><br>
<code>year</code><br>
<code>added</code></p>
<p>Valid <code>sort_order</code> keys are:<br>
<code>asc</code><br>
<code>desc</code></p>
</div><ul class="list-group"><li class="list-group-item bg-default"><strong>Parameters</strong></li><li class="list-group-item"><dl class="dl-horizontal"><dt>username</dt><dd><code>string</code>&nbsp;<span class="required">(required)</span>&nbsp;<span class="text-muted example"><strong>Example:&nbsp;</strong><span>shooezgirl</span></span><p>The username of the submissions you are trying to fetch.</p>
</dd><dt>sort</dt><dd><code>string</code>&nbsp;<span>(optional)</span>&nbsp;<span class="text-muted example"><strong>Example:&nbsp;</strong><span>artist</span></span><p>Sort items by this field (see below for all valid <code>sort</code> keys.</p>
</dd><dt>sort_order</dt><dd><code>string</code>&nbsp;<span>(optional)</span>&nbsp;<span class="text-muted example"><strong>Example:&nbsp;</strong><span>desc</span></span><p>Sort items in a particular order (<code>asc</code> or <code>desc</code>)</p>
</dd></dl></li></ul><ul class="list-group"><li class="list-group-item"><strong>Response&nbsp;&nbsp;<code>200</code></strong><button data-toggle="collapse" data-target="#23c10bed5bcdd20234678919bc781892" type="button" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="23c10bed5bcdd20234678919bc781892" class="pull-right toggle-button">Toggle</button></li><li id="23c10bed5bcdd20234678919bc781892" class="list-group-item panel-collapse collapse"><h5>Body</h5><pre><code>{

  </span>}
</span>}</code></pre></li></ul></section></div></div><a href="#page:user-collection" class="btn btn-default pull-right">Next&nbsp;<i class="fa fa-arrow-circle-right"></i></a><a href="#page:inventory-upload" class="btn btn-default"><i class="fa fa-arrow-circle-left"></i> Previous</a><div class="clearfix"></div><hr></div><div data-bind="visible: page() == 'user-collection', style: {marginTop: page() == 'user-collection' ? '38px' : ''}"><div class="panel panel-default"><div class="panel-heading"><h1 id="user-collection" class="panel-heading-title">User Collection&nbsp;<a href="#page:user-collection"><i class="fa fa-link"></i></a></h1></div><div class="panel-body"><h2 id="user-collection-collection">Collection&nbsp;<a href="#page:user-collection,header:user-collection-collection"><i class="fa fa-link"></i></a></h2><p>The Collection resource allows you to view and manage a user’s collection.<br>
A collection is arranged into folders. Every user has two permanent folders already:</p>
<p>ID <code>0</code>, the “All” folder, which cannot have releases added to it, and<br>
ID <code>1</code>, the “Uncategorized” folder.</p>
<p>Because it’s possible to own more than one copy of a release, each with its own notes, grading, and so on, each instance of a release in a folder has an instance ID.</p>
<p>Through the Discogs website, users can create custom notes fields. There is not yet an API method for creating and deleting these fields, but they can be listed, and the values of the fields on any instance can be modified.</p>
<section id="user-collection-collection-get" class="panel panel-info"><div class="panel-heading"><div style="float:right"><span style="text-transform: lowercase; display: none">Get Collection Folders</span></div><div style="float:left"><a href="#page:user-collection,header:user-collection-collection-get" class="btn btn-xs btn-primary">GET</a></div><div style="overflow:hidden"><code>/users/{username}/collection/folders</code></div></div><div class="panel-body"><p>Retrieve a list of folders in a user’s collection. If the collection has been made private by its owner, <a href="#page:authentication">authentication</a> as the collection owner is required. If you are not authenticated as the collection owner, only folder ID 0 (the “All” folder) will be visible (if the requested user’s collection is public).</p>
</div><ul class="list-group"><li class="list-group-item bg-default"><strong>Parameters</strong></li><li class="list-group-item"><dl class="dl-horizontal"><dt>username</dt><dd><code>string</code>&nbsp;<span class="required">(required)</span>&nbsp;<span class="text-muted example"><strong>Example:&nbsp;</strong><span>rodneyfool</span></span><p>The username of the collection you are trying to retrieve.</p>
</dd></dl></li></ul><ul class="list-group"><li class="list-group-item"><strong>Response&nbsp;&nbsp;<code>200</code></strong><button data-toggle="collapse" data-target="#3ceecdab24338c5cbd2f66e52be016ca" type="button" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="3ceecdab24338c5cbd2f66e52be016ca" class="pull-right toggle-button">Toggle</button></li><li id="3ceecdab24338c5cbd2f66e52be016ca" class="list-group-item panel-collapse collapse"><div class="description"></div><h5>Headers</h5><pre><code><span class="hljs-attribute">Reproxy-Status</span>: <span class="hljs-string">yes</span><br><span class="hljs-attribute">Access-Control-Allow-Origin</span>: <span class="hljs-string">*</span><br><span class="hljs-attribute">Cache-Control</span>: <span class="hljs-string">public, must-revalidate</span><br><span class="hljs-attribute">Content-Type</span>: <span class="hljs-string">application/json</span><br><span class="hljs-attribute">Server</span>: <span class="hljs-string">lighttpd</span><br><span class="hljs-attribute">Content-Length</span>: <span class="hljs-string">132</span><br><span class="hljs-attribute">Date</span>: <span class="hljs-string">Wed, 16 Jul 2014 23:20:21 GMT</span><br><span class="hljs-attribute">X-Varnish</span>: <span class="hljs-string">1722533701</span><br><span class="hljs-attribute">Age</span>: <span class="hljs-string">0</span><br><span class="hljs-attribute">Via</span>: <span class="hljs-string">1.1 varnish</span><br><span class="hljs-attribute">Connection</span>: <span class="hljs-string">keep-alive</span><br></code></pre><h5>Body</h5><pre><code>{
  "<span class="hljs-attribute">folders</span>": <span class="hljs-value">[
    {
      "<span class="hljs-attribute">id</span>": <span class="hljs-value"><span class="hljs-number">0</span></span>,
      "<span class="hljs-attribute">count</span>": <span class="hljs-value"><span class="hljs-number">23</span></span>,
      "<span class="hljs-attribute">name</span>": <span class="hljs-value"><span class="hljs-string">"All"</span></span>,
      "<span class="hljs-attribute">resource_url</span>": <span class="hljs-value"><span class="hljs-string">"https://api.discogs.com/users/example/collection/folders/0"</span>
    </span>},
    {
      "<span class="hljs-attribute">id</span>": <span class="hljs-value"><span class="hljs-number">1</span></span>,
      "<span class="hljs-attribute">count</span>": <span class="hljs-value"><span class="hljs-number">20</span></span>,
      "<span class="hljs-attribute">name</span>": <span class="hljs-value"><span class="hljs-string">"Uncategorized"</span></span>,
      "<span class="hljs-attribute">resource_url</span>": <span class="hljs-value"><span class="hljs-string">"https://api.discogs.com/users/example/collection/folders/1"</span>
    </span>}
  ]
</span>}</code></pre></li></ul></section><section id="user-collection-collection-post" class="panel panel-success"><div class="panel-heading"><div style="float:right"><span style="text-transform: lowercase; display: none">Create Folder</span></div><div style="float:left"><a href="#page:user-collection,header:user-collection-collection-post" class="btn btn-xs btn-success">POST</a></div><div style="overflow:hidden"><code>/users/{username}/collection/folders</code></div></div><div class="panel-body"><p>Create a new folder in a user’s collection.</p>
<p><a href="#page:authentication">Authentication</a> as the collection owner is required.</p>
</div><ul class="list-group"><li class="list-group-item bg-default"><strong>Parameters</strong></li><li class="list-group-item"><dl class="dl-horizontal"><dt>username</dt><dd><code>string</code>&nbsp;<span class="required">(required)</span>&nbsp;<span class="text-muted example"><strong>Example:&nbsp;</strong><span>rodneyfool</span></span><p>The username of the collection you are trying to retrieve.</p>
</dd><dt>name</dt><dd><code>string</code>&nbsp;<span>(optional)</span>&nbsp;<span class="text-muted example"><strong>Example:&nbsp;</strong><span>My favorites</span></span><p>The name of the newly-created folder.</p>
</dd></dl></li></ul><ul class="list-group"><li class="list-group-item"><strong>Response&nbsp;&nbsp;<code>201</code></strong><button data-toggle="collapse" data-target="#e616e5f79e2f6bfff3bd0d8986ebdbd4" type="button" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="e616e5f79e2f6bfff3bd0d8986ebdbd4" class="pull-right toggle-button">Toggle</button></li><li id="e616e5f79e2f6bfff3bd0d8986ebdbd4" class="list-group-item panel-collapse collapse"><h5>Body</h5><pre><code>{
  "<span class="hljs-attribute">id</span>": <span class="hljs-value"><span class="hljs-number">232842</span></span>,
  "<span class="hljs-attribute">name</span>": <span class="hljs-value"><span class="hljs-string">"My Music"</span></span>,
  "<span class="hljs-attribute">count</span>": <span class="hljs-value"><span class="hljs-number">0</span></span>,
  "<span class="hljs-attribute">resource_url</span>": <span class="hljs-value"><span class="hljs-string">"https://api.discogs.com/users/example/collection/folders/232842"</span>
</span>}</code></pre></li></ul></section><h2 id="user-collection-collection-folder">Collection Folder&nbsp;<a href="#page:user-collection,header:user-collection-collection-folder"><i class="fa fa-link"></i></a></h2><section id="user-collection-collection-folder-get" class="panel panel-info"><div class="panel-heading"><div style="float:right"><span style="text-transform: lowercase; display: none">Get Folders</span></div><div style="float:left"><a href="#page:user-collection,header:user-collection-collection-folder-get" class="btn btn-xs btn-primary">GET</a></div><div style="overflow:hidden"><code>/users/{username}/collection/folders/{folder_id}</code></div></div><div class="panel-body"><p>Retrieve metadata about a folder in a user’s collection.</p>
<p>If <code>folder_id</code> is not <code>0</code>, <a href="#page:authentication">authentication</a> as the collection owner is required.</p>
</div><ul class="list-group"><li class="list-group-item bg-default"><strong>Parameters</strong></li><li class="list-group-item"><dl class="dl-horizontal"><dt>username</dt><dd><code>string</code>&nbsp;<span class="required">(required)</span>&nbsp;<span class="text-muted example"><strong>Example:&nbsp;</strong><span>rodneyfool</span></span><p>The username of the collection you are trying to request.</p>
</dd><dt>folder_id</dt><dd><code>number</code>&nbsp;<span class="required">(required)</span>&nbsp;<span class="text-muted example"><strong>Example:&nbsp;</strong><span>3</span></span><p>The ID of the folder to request.</p>
</dd></dl></li></ul><ul class="list-group"><li class="list-group-item"><strong>Response&nbsp;&nbsp;<code>200</code></strong><button data-toggle="collapse" data-target="#36acaf1518b0454842a2f27cf11fe69d" type="button" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="36acaf1518b0454842a2f27cf11fe69d" class="pull-right toggle-button">Toggle</button></li><li id="36acaf1518b0454842a2f27cf11fe69d" class="list-group-item panel-collapse collapse"><div class="description"></div><h5>Headers</h5><pre><code><span class="hljs-attribute">Reproxy-Status</span>: <span class="hljs-string">yes</span><br><span class="hljs-attribute">Access-Control-Allow-Origin</span>: <span class="hljs-string">*</span><br><span class="hljs-attribute">Cache-Control</span>: <span class="hljs-string">public, must-revalidate</span><br><span class="hljs-attribute">Content-Type</span>: <span class="hljs-string">application/json</span><br><span class="hljs-attribute">Server</span>: <span class="hljs-string">lighttpd</span><br><span class="hljs-attribute">Content-Length</span>: <span class="hljs-string">132</span><br><span class="hljs-attribute">Date</span>: <span class="hljs-string">Wed, 16 Jul 2014 23:20:21 GMT</span><br><span class="hljs-attribute">X-Varnish</span>: <span class="hljs-string">1722533701</span><br><span class="hljs-attribute">Age</span>: <span class="hljs-string">0</span><br><span class="hljs-attribute">Via</span>: <span class="hljs-string">1.1 varnish</span><br><span class="hljs-attribute">Connection</span>: <span class="hljs-string">keep-alive</span><br></code></pre><h5>Body</h5><pre><code>{
  "<span class="hljs-attribute">id</span>": <span class="hljs-value"><span class="hljs-number">1</span></span>,

  "<span class="hljs-attribute">name</span>": <span class="hljs-value"><span class="hljs-string">"Uncategorized"</span></span>,

</span>}</code></pre></li></ul></section><section id="user-collection-collection-folder-post" class="panel panel-success"><div class="panel-heading"><div style="float:right"><span style="text-transform: lowercase; display: none">Edit Folder</span></div><div style="float:left"><a href="#page:user-collection,header:user-collection-collection-folder-post" class="btn btn-xs btn-success">POST</a></div><div style="overflow:hidden"><code>/users/{username}/collection/folders/{folder_id}</code></div></div><div class="panel-body"><p>Edit a folder’s metadata. Folders <code>0</code> and <code>1</code> cannot be renamed.</p>
<p><a href="#page:authentication">Authentication</a> as the collection owner is required.</p>
</div><ul class="list-group"><li class="list-group-item bg-default"><strong>Parameters</strong></li><li class="list-group-item"><dl class="dl-horizontal"><dt>username</dt><dd><code>string</code>&nbsp;<span class="required">(required)</span>&nbsp;<span class="text-muted example"><strong>Example:&nbsp;</strong><span>rodneyfool</span></span><p>The username of the collection you are trying to modify.</p>
</dd><dt>folder_id</dt><dd><code>number</code>&nbsp;<span class="required">(required)</span>&nbsp;<span class="text-muted example"><strong>Example:&nbsp;</strong><span>3</span></span><p>The ID of the folder to modify.</p>
</dd></dl></li></ul><ul class="list-group"><li class="list-group-item"><strong>Response&nbsp;&nbsp;<code>200</code></strong><button data-toggle="collapse" data-target="#6e7a104a32017ba1a7be4fb9552b9853" type="button" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="6e7a104a32017ba1a7be4fb9552b9853" class="pull-right toggle-button">Toggle</button></li><li id="6e7a104a32017ba1a7be4fb9552b9853" class="list-group-item panel-collapse collapse"><h5>Body</h5><pre><code>{

  "<span class="hljs-attribute">name</span>": <span class="hljs-value"><span class="hljs-string">"An Example Folder"</span></span>,
  "<span class="hljs-attribute">resource_url</span>": <span class="hljs-value"><span class="hljs-string">"https://api.discogs.com/users/example/collection/folders/392"</span>
</span>}</code></pre></li></ul></section><section id="user-collection-collection-folder-delete" class="panel panel-danger"><div class="panel-heading"><div style="float:right"><span style="text-transform: lowercase; display: none">Delete Folder</span></div><div style="float:left"><a href="#page:user-collection,header:user-collection-collection-folder-delete" class="btn btn-xs btn-danger">DELETE</a></div><div style="overflow:hidden"><code>/users/{username}/collection/folders/{folder_id}</code></div></div><div class="panel-body"><p>Delete a folder from a user’s collection. A folder must be empty before it can be deleted.</p>
<p><a href="#page:authentication">Authentication</a> as the collection owner is required.</p>
</div><ul class="list-group"><li class="list-group-item bg-default"><strong>Parameters</strong></li><li class="list-group-item"><dl class="dl-horizontal"><dt>username</dt><dd><code>string</code>&nbsp;<span class="required">(required)</span>&nbsp;<span class="text-muted example"><strong>Example:&nbsp;</strong><span>rodneyfool</span></span><p>The username of the collection you are trying to modify.</p>
</dd><dt>folder_id</dt><dd><code>number</code>&nbsp;<span class="required">(required)</span>&nbsp;<span class="text-muted example"><strong>Example:&nbsp;</strong><span>3</span></span><p>The ID of the folder to delete.</p>
</dd></dl></li></ul><ul class="list-group"><li class="list-group-item"><strong>Response&nbsp;&nbsp;<code>204</code></strong></li></ul></section><h2 id="user-collection-collection-items-by-release">Collection Items By Release&nbsp;<a href="#page:user-collection,header:user-collection-collection-items-by-release"><i class="fa fa-link"></i></a></h2><section id="user-collection-collection-items-by-release-get" class="panel panel-info"><div class="panel-heading"><div style="float:right"><span style="text-transform: lowercase; display: none">Get Items By Release</span></div><div style="float:left"><a href="#page:user-collection,header:user-collection-collection-items-by-release-get" class="btn btn-xs btn-primary">GET</a></div><div style="overflow:hidden"><code>/users/{username}/collection/releases/{release_id}</code></div></div><div class="panel-body"><p>View the user’s collection folders which contain a specified release. This will
also show information about each release instance.</p>
<p>The <code>release_id</code> must be non-zero.</p>
<p><a href="#page:authentication">Authentication</a> as the collection owner
is required if the owner’s collection is private.</p>
</div><ul class="list-group"><li class="list-group-item bg-default"><strong>Parameters</strong></li><li class="list-group-item"><dl class="dl-horizontal"><dt>username</dt><dd><code>string</code>&nbsp;<span class="required">(required)</span>&nbsp;<span class="text-muted example"><strong>Example:&nbsp;</strong><span>susan.salkeld</span></span><p>The username of the collection you are trying to view.</p>
</dd><dt>release_id</dt><dd><code>number</code>&nbsp;<span class="required">(required)</span>&nbsp;<span class="text-muted example"><strong>Example:&nbsp;</strong><span>7781525</span></span><p>The ID of the release to request.</p>

Accepts <a href="#page:home,header:home-pagination">Pagination</a> parameters.</p>
<p>Basic information about each release is provided, suitable for display in a list. For detailed information, make another API call to fetch the corresponding release.</p>
<p>If <code>folder_id</code> is not <code>0</code>, or the collection has been made private by its owner, <a href="#page:authentication">authentication</a> as the collection owner is required.</p>
<p>If you are not authenticated as the collection owner, only public notes fields will be visible.</p>
<p>Valid <code>sort</code> keys are:<br>
<code>label</code><br>
<code>artist</code><br>
<code>title</code><br>
<code>catno</code><br>
<code>format</code><br>
<code>rating</code><br>
<code>added</code><br>
<code>year</code></p>
</div><ul class="list-group"><li class="list-group-item bg-default"><strong>Parameters</strong></li><li class="list-group-item"><dl class="dl-horizontal"><dt>username</dt><dd><code>string</code>&nbsp;<span class="required">(required)</span>&nbsp;<span class="text-muted example"><strong>Example:&nbsp;</strong><span>rodneyfool</span></span><p>The username of the collection you are trying to request.</p>
</dd><dt>folder_id</dt><dd><code>number</code>&nbsp;<span class="required">(required)</span>&nbsp;<span class="text-muted example"><strong>Example:&nbsp;</strong><span>3</span></span><p>The ID of the folder to request.</p>
</dd><dt>sort</dt><dd><code>string</code>&nbsp;<span>(optional)</span>&nbsp;<span class="text-muted example"><strong>Example:&nbsp;</strong><span>artist</span></span><p>Sort items by this field (see below for all valid <code>sort</code> keys.</p>
</dd><dt>sort_order</dt><dd><code>string</code>&nbsp;<span>(optional)</span>&nbsp;<span class="text-muted example"><strong>Example:&nbsp;</strong><span>desc</span></span><p>Sort items in a particular order (<code>asc</code> or <code>desc</code>)</p>
</dd></dl></li></ul><ul class="list-group"><li class="list-group-item"><strong>Response&nbsp;&nbsp;<code>200</code></strong><button data-toggle="collapse" data-target="#477a31937687f117b075124d99e49e86" type="button" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="477a31937687f117b075124d99e49e86" class="pull-right toggle-button">Toggle</button></li><li id="477a31937687f117b075124d99e49e86" class="list-group-item panel-collapse collapse"><div class="description"></div><h5>Headers</h5><pre><code><span class="hljs-attribute">Reproxy-Status</span>: <span class="hljs-string">yes</span><br><span class="hljs-attribute">Access-Control-Allow-Origin</span>: <span class="hljs-string">*</span><br><span class="hljs-attribute">Cache-Control</span>: <span class="hljs-string">public, must-revalidate</span><br><span class="hljs-attribute">Content-Type</span>: <span class="hljs-string">application/json</span><br><span class="hljs-attribute">Server</span>: <span class="hljs-string">lighttpd</span><br><span class="hljs-attribute">Content-Length</span>: <span class="hljs-string">132</span><br><span class="hljs-attribute">Date</span>: <span class="hljs-string">Wed, 16 Jul 2014 23:20:21 GMT</span><br><span class="hljs-attribute">X-Varnish</span>: <span class="hljs-string">1722533701</span><br><span class="hljs-attribute">Age</span>: <span class="hljs-string">0</span><br><span class="hljs-attribute">Via</span>: <span class="hljs-string">1.1 varnish</span><br><span class="hljs-attribute">Connection</span>: <span class="hljs-string">keep-alive</span><br></code></pre><h5>Body</h5><pre><code>{

<p>The <code>folder_id</code> must be non-zero – you can use <code>1</code> for “Uncategorized”.</p>
<p><a href="#page:authentication">Authentication</a> as the collection owner is required.</p>
</div><ul class="list-group"><li class="list-group-item bg-default"><strong>Parameters</strong></li><li class="list-group-item"><dl class="dl-horizontal"><dt>username</dt><dd><code>string</code>&nbsp;<span class="required">(required)</span>&nbsp;<span class="text-muted example"><strong>Example:&nbsp;</strong><span>rodneyfool</span></span><p>The username of the collection you are trying to modify.</p>
</dd><dt>folder_id</dt><dd><code>number</code>&nbsp;<span class="required">(required)</span>&nbsp;<span class="text-muted example"><strong>Example:&nbsp;</strong><span>3</span></span><p>The ID of the folder to modify.</p>
</dd><dt>release_id</dt><dd><code>number</code>&nbsp;<span class="required">(required)</span>&nbsp;<span class="text-muted example"><strong>Example:&nbsp;</strong><span>130076</span></span><p>The ID of the release you are adding.</p>
</dd></dl></li></ul><ul class="list-group"><li class="list-group-item"><strong>Response&nbsp;&nbsp;<code>201</code></strong><button data-toggle="collapse" data-target="#9b993a098872966d080ea79b483ab704" type="button" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="9b993a098872966d080ea79b483ab704" class="pull-right toggle-button">Toggle</button></li><li id="9b993a098872966d080ea79b483ab704" class="list-group-item panel-collapse collapse"><h5>Body</h5><pre><code>{
  "<span class="hljs-attribute">instance_id</span>": <span class="hljs-value"><span class="hljs-number">3</span></span>,
  "<span class="hljs-attribute">resource_url</span>": <span class="hljs-value"><span class="hljs-string">"https://api.discogs.com/users/example/collection/folders/1/release/1/instance/3"</span>
</span>}</code></pre></li></ul></section><h2 id="user-collection-change-rating-of-release">Change Rating Of Release&nbsp;<a href="#page:user-collection,header:user-collection-change-rating-of-release"><i class="fa fa-link"></i></a></h2><section id="user-collection-change-rating-of-release-post" class="panel panel-success"><div class="panel-heading"><div style="float:right"><span style="text-transform: lowercase; display: none">Change Rating</span></div><div style="float:left"><a href="#page:user-collection,header:user-collection-change-rating-of-release-post" class="btn btn-xs btn-success">POST</a></div><div style="overflow:hidden"><code>/users/{username}/collection/folders/{folder_id}/releases/{release_id}/instances/{instance_id}</code></div></div><div class="panel-body"><p>Change the rating on a release and/or move the instance to another folder.</p>
<p>This endpoint potentially takes 2 <code>folder_id</code> parameters: one in the URL (which
is the folder you are requesting, and is required), and one in the
request body (representing the folder you want to move the instance to, which is
optional)</p>
<p><a href="#page:authentication">Authentication</a> as the collection owner is required.</p>
</div><ul class="list-group"><li class="list-group-item bg-default"><strong>Parameters</strong></li><li class="list-group-item"><dl class="dl-horizontal"><dt>username</dt><dd><code>string</code>&nbsp;<span class="required">(required)</span>&nbsp;<span class="text-muted example"><strong>Example:&nbsp;</strong><span>rodneyfool</span></span><p>The username of the collection you are trying to modify.</p>
</dd><dt>folder_id</dt><dd><code>number</code>&nbsp;<span>(optional)</span>&nbsp;<span class="text-muted example"><strong>Example:&nbsp;</strong><span>4</span></span><p>The ID of the folder to modify (this parameter is set in the request body and is set if you want to move the instance to this folder).</p>
</dd><dt>release_id</dt><dd><code>number</code>&nbsp;<span class="required">(required)</span>&nbsp;<span class="text-muted example"><strong>Example:&nbsp;</strong><span>130076</span></span><p>The ID of the release you are modifying.</p>
</dd><dt>instance_id</dt><dd><code>number</code>&nbsp;<span class="required">(required)</span>&nbsp;<span class="text-muted example"><strong>Example:&nbsp;</strong><span>1</span></span><p>The ID of the instance.</p>
</dd><dt>rating</dt><dd><code>number</code>&nbsp;<span>(optional)</span>&nbsp;<span class="text-muted example"><strong>Example:&nbsp;</strong><span>5</span></span><p>The rating of the instance you are supplying.</p>
</dd></dl></li></ul><ul class="list-group"><li class="list-group-item"><strong>Response&nbsp;&nbsp;<code>204</code></strong></li></ul></section><h2 id="user-collection-delete-instance-from-folder">Delete Instance From Folder&nbsp;<a href="#page:user-collection,header:user-collection-delete-instance-from-folder"><i class="fa fa-link"></i></a></h2><section id="user-collection-delete-instance-from-folder-delete" class="panel panel-danger"><div class="panel-heading"><div style="float:right"><span style="text-transform: lowercase; display: none">Delete Instance</span></div><div style="float:left"><a href="#page:user-collection,header:user-collection-delete-instance-from-folder-delete" class="btn btn-xs btn-danger">DELETE</a></div><div style="overflow:hidden"><code>/users/{username}/collection/folders/{folder_id}/releases/{release_id}/instances/{instance_id}</code></div></div><div class="panel-body"><p>Remove an instance of a release from a user’s collection folder.</p>
<p>To move the release to the “Uncategorized” folder instead, use the <code>POST</code> method.</p>
<p><a href="#page:authentication">Authentication</a> as the collection owner is required.</p>
</div><ul class="list-group"><li class="list-group-item bg-default"><strong>Parameters</strong></li><li class="list-group-item"><dl class="dl-horizontal"><dt>username</dt><dd><code>string</code>&nbsp;<span class="required">(required)</span>&nbsp;<span class="text-muted example"><strong>Example:&nbsp;</strong><span>rodneyfool</span></span><p>The username of the collection you are trying to modify.</p>
</dd><dt>folder_id</dt><dd><code>number</code>&nbsp;<span class="required">(required)</span>&nbsp;<span class="text-muted example"><strong>Example:&nbsp;</strong><span>3</span></span><p>The ID of the folder to modify.</p>
</dd><dt>release_id</dt><dd><code>number</code>&nbsp;<span class="required">(required)</span>&nbsp;<span class="text-muted example"><strong>Example:&nbsp;</strong><span>130076</span></span><p>The ID of the release you are modifying.</p>
</dd><dt>instance_id</dt><dd><code>number</code>&nbsp;<span class="required">(required)</span>&nbsp;<span class="text-muted example"><strong>Example:&nbsp;</strong><span>1</span></span><p>The ID of the instance.</p>
</dd></dl></li></ul><ul class="list-group"><li class="list-group-item"><strong>Response&nbsp;&nbsp;<code>204</code></strong></li><li class="list-group-item"><strong>Response&nbsp;&nbsp;<code>403</code></strong><button data-toggle="collapse" data-target="#b36d56c6d74e2f90f4029957712b34cd" type="button" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="b36d56c6d74e2f90f4029957712b34cd" class="pull-right toggle-button">Toggle</button></li><li id="b36d56c6d74e2f90f4029957712b34cd" class="list-group-item panel-collapse collapse"><h5>Body</h5><pre><code>{
  "<span class="hljs-attribute">message</span>": <span class="hljs-value"><span class="hljs-string">"You don't have permission to access this resource."</span>
</span>}</code></pre></li></ul></section><h2 id="user-collection-list-custom-fields">List Custom Fields&nbsp;<a href="#page:user-collection,header:user-collection-list-custom-fields"><i class="fa fa-link"></i></a></h2><section id="user-collection-list-custom-fields-get" class="panel panel-info"><div class="panel-heading"><div style="float:right"><span style="text-transform: lowercase; display: none">List Fields</span></div><div style="float:left"><a href="#page:user-collection,header:user-collection-list-custom-fields-get" class="btn btn-xs btn-primary">GET</a></div><div style="overflow:hidden"><code>/users/{username}/collection/fields</code></div></div><div class="panel-body"><p>Retrieve a list of user-defined collection notes fields. '38px' : ''}"><div class="panel panel-default"><div class="panel-heading"><h1 id="user-wantlist" class="panel-heading-title">User Wantlist&nbsp;<a href="#page:user-wantlist"><i class="fa fa-link"></i></a></h1></div><div class="panel-body"><h2 id="user-wantlist-wantlist">Wantlist&nbsp;<a href="#page:user-wantlist,header:user-wantlist-wantlist"><i class="fa fa-link"></i></a></h2><p>The Wantlist resource allows you to view and manage a user’s wantlist.</p>
<section id="user-wantlist-wantlist-get" class="panel panel-info"><div class="panel-heading"><div style="float:right"><span style="text-transform: lowercase; display: none">Get Wantlist</span></div><div style="float:left"><a href="#page:user-wantlist,header:user-wantlist-wantlist-get" class="btn btn-xs btn-primary">GET</a></div><div style="overflow:hidden"><code>/users/{username}/wants</code></div></div><div class="panel-body"><p>Returns the list of releases in a user’s wantlist. Accepts <a href="#page:home,header:home-pagination">Pagination</a> parameters.</p>
<p>Basic information about each release is provided, suitable for display in a list. For detailed information, make another API call to fetch the corresponding release.</p>

<p>The <code>notes</code> field will be visible if you are authenticated as the wantlist owner.</p>

<p><a href="#page:authentication">Authentication</a> as the wantlist owner is required.</p>
<section id="user-wantlist-add-to-wantlist-put" class="panel panel-warning"><div class="panel-heading"><div style="float:right"><span style="text-transform: lowercase; display: none">Add To Wantlist</span></div><div style="float:left"><a href="#page:user-wantlist,header:user-wantlist-add-to-wantlist-put" class="btn btn-xs btn-warning">PUT</a></div><div style="overflow:hidden"><code>/users/{username}/wants/{release_id}{?notes,rating}</code></div></div><ul class="list-group"><li class="list-group-item bg-default"><strong>Parameters</strong></li><li class="list-group-item"><dl class="dl-horizontal"><dt>username</dt><dd><code>string</code>&nbsp;<span class="required">(required)</span>&nbsp;<span class="text-muted example"><strong>Example:&nbsp;</strong><span>rodneyfool</span></span><p>The username of the wantlist you are trying to fetch.</p>
</dd><dt>release_id</dt><dd><code>number</code>&nbsp;<span class="required">(required)</span>&nbsp;<span class="text-muted example"><strong>Example:&nbsp;</strong><span>130076</span></span><p>The ID of the release you are adding.</p>

</script><script src="//cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/knockout/3.0.0/knockout-min.js"></script><script>(function() {
  var App;

  App = (function() {
    function App() {
      this.page = ko.observable('home');
    }

    return App;

  })();

  window.app = new App();

  window.onhashchange = function() {
    var i, isNarrowViewport, len, mobileBreakpoint, parts, ref, v, vars;
    vars = {};
    ref = location.hash.substr(1).split(',');
    for (i = 0, len = ref.length; i < len; i++) {
      v = ref[i];
      parts = v.split(':');
      vars[parts[0]] = parts[1];
    }
    window.app.page(vars.page || 'home');
    if (vars.page) {
      vars.page = vars.page.split('-').map(function(word) {
        return word.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + word.substring(1);
      }).join(' ');
      document.title = vars.page[0].toUpperCase() + vars.page.substring(1) + ' - Discogs API Documentation';
    } else {
      document.title = 'Home - Discogs API Documentation';
    }
    mobileBreakpoint = 990;
    isNarrowViewport = $(window).width() < mobileBreakpoint;
    if (vars.header) {
      return $("#" + vars.header)[0].scrollIntoView(true);
    } else if (isNarrowViewport && vars.page) {
      return $("#" + vars.page).parents('.panel')[0].scrollIntoView(true);
    } else {
      return window.scrollTo(0, 0);
    }
  };

  ko.applyBindings(window.app);

  window.onhashchange();

}).call(this);
</script></html>
